`1|To Kill a Mockingbird|Harper Lee|978-0-06-112008-4|Fiction|HarperCollins|1960|A gripping tale of racial injustice and childhood innocence.|Available|4.8`\n  - `2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|978-0-06-231609-7|Non-Fiction|Harper|2011|A brief history of humankind.|Borrowed|4.6`\n  - `borrow_id` (int)\n  - `username` (str)\n  - `book_id` (int)\n  - `borrow_date` (str) (format YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - `due_date` (str) (format YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - `return_date` (str or empty) (format YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - `status` (str) - \"Active\", \"Returned\", \"Overdue\"\n  - `fine_amount` (float)\n- Description: Records borrow transactions and status.\n- Example Rows:\n  - `1|john_reader|2|2024-11-01|2024-11-15||Active|0`\n  - 'All')\n    borrowings = read_borrowings()\n    books = read_books()\n\n    filtered_borrows = []\n    for b in borrowings:\n        if b['username'] != CURRENT_USERNAME:\n            continue\n        # Filter by status if not 'All'\n        if filter_status != 'All' and b['status'] != filter_status:\n            continue\n        # Get book title\n        book_title = next((bk['title'] for bk in books if bk['book_id'] == b['book_id']), 'Unknown')\n        borrow_entry = {\n            'borrow_id': b['borrow_id'],\n            'book_title': book_title,\n            'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],\n            'due_date': b['due_date'],\n            'status': b['status']\n        }\n        filtered_borrows.append(borrow_entry)\n\n    return render_template('my_borrows.html', borrows=filtered_borrows, filter_status=filter_status)\n\n\n@app.route('/return/<int:borrow_id>', methods=['POST'])\ndef return_book(borrow_id):\n    borrowings = read_borrowings()\n    borrow_found = False\n    for b in borrowings:\n        if b['borrow_id'] == borrow_id and b['username'] == CURRENT_USERNAME:\n            if b['status'] not in ['Active', 'Overdue']:\n                flash('Borrow record not active or already returned.')\n                return redirect(url_for('my_borrows'))\n            b['return_date'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n            b['status'] = 'Returned'\n            b['fine_amount'] = 0.0\n            borrow_found = True\n            # Update book status to Available\n            update_book_status(b['book_id'], 'Available')\n            break\n    if borrow_found:\n        write_borrowings(borrowings)\n        flash('Book returned successfully.')\n    else:\n        flash('Borrow record not found.')\n\n    return    return render_template('write_review.html', review=review_context)\n\n\n@app.route('/edit_review/<int:review_id>/submit', methods=['POST'])\ndef submit_edit_review(review_id):\n    rating = raise ValueError\n    except ValueError:\n        flash('Invalid rating value.')\n        return redirect(url_for('write_review_page', book_id=book_id))\n\n    reviews_all = read_reviews()\n    new_review_id = next_review_id()\n    new_review = {\n        'review_id': new_review_id,\n        'username': CURRENT_USERNAME,\n        'book_id': book_id,\n        'rating': rating_val,\n        'review_text': review_text,\n        'review_date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n    }\n    reviews_all.append(new_review)\n    write_reviews(reviews_all)\n\n    flash('Review submitted successfully.')\n    return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))\n\n\n@app.route('/profile')\ndef user_profile():\n    user = find_user(CURRENT_USERNAME)\n    if not user:\n        flash('User not found.')\n        return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))\n\n    borrowings = read_borrowings()\n    books = read_books()\n\n    borrow_history = []\n    for b in borrowings:\n        if return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    app.run(debug=True)\n\n\n=== lang=\"en\">\n<head>\n    <meta charset=\"UTF-8\">\n    <title>Write Review</title>\n</head>\n<body>\n<div id=\"write-review-page\">\n    <h1>Write Review</h1>\n    <form method=\"POST\" action=\"{{ url_for('submit_edit_review', review_id=review.review_id) if review else url_for('submit_write_review', book_id=book_id) }}\">\n        <label for=\"rating-input\">Rating:</label>\n        <input id=\"rating-input\" name=\"rating\" type=\"number\" min=\"1\" max=\"5\" value=\"{{ review.rating if review else '' }}\" required>\n        <label for=\"review-textarea\">Review Text:</label>\n        <textarea id=\"review-textarea\" name=\"review_text\" required>{{ review.review_text if review else '' }}</textarea>\n        <button id=\"submit-review-button\" type=\"submit\">Submit Review</button>\n    </form>\n    <a href=\"{{ url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id) }}\" id=\"back-to-book\">Back to Book</a>\n</div>\n</body>\n</html>\n\n=== design_spec.md ===\n# Design Specification Document for OnlineLibrary\n\n---\n\n## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (Backend Development)\n\n### 1. Root Route\n- URL Path: `/`\n- Function Name: `root_redirect`\n- HTTP Method: GET\n- Template Rendered: Redirect to `dashboard`\n- Context Variables: None\n\n### 2. Dashboard Page\n- URL Path: `/dashboard`\n- Function Name: `dashboard`\n- HTTP Method: GET\n- Template Rendered: `dashboard.html`\n- Context Variables:\n  - `username` (str): Logged-in user's username\n  - `featured_books` (list of dict): List of featured books on dashboard; each dict with keys:\n    - `book_id` (int)\n    - `title` (str)\n    - `author` (str)\n    - `status` (str) - one of \"Available\", \"Borrowed\", \"Reserved\"\n\n### 3. Book Catalog Page\n- URL Path: `/catalog`\n- Function Name: `book_catalog`\n- HTTP Method: GET\n- Template Rendered: `catalog.html`\n- Context Variables:\n  - `books` (list of dict): List of books; each dict has keys:\n    - `book_id` (int)\n    - `title` (str)\n    - `author` (str)\n    - `status` (str)\n\n### 4. Book Details Page\n- URL Path: `/book/<int:book_id>`\n- Function Name: `book_details`\n- HTTP Method: GET\n- Template Rendered: `book_details.html`\n- Context Variables:\n  - `book` (dict): Book information with keys:\n    - `book_id` (int)\n    - `title` (str)\n    - `author` (str)\n    - `status` (str)\n    - `description` (str)\n    - `avg_rating` (float)\n  - `reviews` (list of dict): List of review dicts with keys:\n    - `review_id` (int)\n    - `username` (str)\n    - `rating` (int)\n    - `review_text` (str)\n    - `review_date` (str) (format YYYY-MM-DD)\n\n### 5. Borrow Confirmation Page\n- URL Path: `/borrow/<int:book_id>`\n- Function Name: `borrow_confirmation`\n- HTTP Method: GET\n- Template Rendered: `borrow.html`\n- Context Variables:\n  - `book` (dict): Book info as in `book_details`\n  - `due_date` (str): Due date string 14 days from current date (format YYYY-MM-DD)\n\n- URL Path: `/borrow/<int:book_id>/confirm`\n- Function Name: `confirm_borrow`\n- HTTP Method: POST\n- Template Rendered: Redirect or confirmation page as needed (not rendering borrow.html again)\n- Context Variables: None\n\n- URL Path: `/borrow/<int:book_id>/cancel`\n- Function Name: `cancel_borrow`\n- HTTP Method: POST\n- Template Rendered: Redirect to `book_details` page\n- Context Variables: None\n\n### 6. My Borrowings Page\n- URL Path: `/my_borrows`\n- Function Name: `my_borrows`\n- HTTP Method: GET\n- Template Rendered: `my_borrows.html`\n- Context Variables:\n  - `borrows` (list of dict): List of borrowings with keys:\n    - `borrow_id` (int)\n    - `book_title` (str)\n    - `borrow_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)\n    - `due_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)\n    - `status` (str) - e.g., Active, Returned, Overdue\n  - `filter_status` (str): The current filter selected (All, Active, Returned, Overdue)\n\n- URL Path: `/return/<int:borrow_id>`\n- Function Name: `return_book`\n- HTTP Method: POST\n- Template Rendered: Redirect or confirmation page\n- Context Variables: None\n\n### 7. My Reservations Page\n- URL Path: `/my_reservations`\n- Function Name: `my_reservations`\n- HTTP Method: GET\n- Template Rendered: `my_reservations.html`\n- Context Variables:\n  - `reservations` (list of dict): List of reservations with keys:\n    - `reservation_id` (int)\n    - `book_title` (str)\n    - `reservation_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)\n    - `status` (str) - e.g., Active, Cancelled\n\n- URL Path: `/cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id>`\n- Function Name: `cancel_reservation`\n- HTTP Method: POST\n- Template Rendered: Redirect or confirmation\n- Context Variables: None\n\n### 8. My Reviews Page\n- URL Path: `/my_reviews`\n- Function Name: `my_reviews`\n- HTTP Method: GET\n- Template Rendered: `my_reviews.html`\n- Context Variables:\n  - `reviews` (list of dict): List of user reviews with keys:\n    - `review_id` (int)\n    - `book_title` (str)\n    - `rating` (int)\n    - `review_text` (str)\n\n- URL Path: `/edit_review/<int:review_id>`\n- Function Name: `edit_review_page`\n- HTTP Method: GET\n- Template Rendered: `write_review.html`\n- Context Variables:\n  - `review` (dict): Existing review details with keys:\n    - `review_id` (int)\n    - `book_id` (int)\n    - `rating` (int)\n    - `review_text` (str)\n    - `book_title` (str)\n\n- URL Path: `/edit_review/<int:review_id>/submit`\n- Function Name: `submit_edit_review`\n- HTTP Method: POST\n- Template Rendered: Redirect to `my_reviews` or confirmation\n- Context Variables: None\n\n- URL Path: `/delete_review/<int:review_id>`\n- Function Name: `delete_review`\n- HTTP Method: POST\n- Template Rendered: Redirect to `my_reviews`\n- Context Variables: None\n\n### 9. Write Review Page\n- URL Path: `/write_review/<int:book_id>`\n- Function Name: `write_review_page`\n- HTTP Method: GET\n- Template Rendered: `write_review.html`\n- Context Variables:\n  - `book` (dict): Book info with keys:\n    - `book_id` (int)\n    - `title` (str)\n    - `author` (str)\n\n- URL Path: `/write_review/<int:book_id>/submit`\n- Function Name: `submit_review`\n- HTTP Method: POST\n- Template Rendered: Redirect to book details or confirmation\n- Context Variables: None\n\n### 10. User Profile Page\n- URL Path: `/profile`\n- Function Name: `user_profile`\n- HTTP Method: GET\n- Template Rendered: `profile.html`\n- Context Variables:\n  - `username` (str)\n  - `email` (str)\n  - `borrow_history` (list of dict): List of previously borrowed books with keys:\n    - `book_title` (str)\n    - `borrow_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)\n    - `return_date` (str or None)\n\n- URL Path: `/profile/update`\n- Function Name: `update_profile`\n- HTTP Method: POST\n- Template Rendered: Redirect or confirmation\n- Context Variables: None\n\n### 11. Write Review Template\n- Filename: `templates/write_review.html`\n- Page Title: \"Write Review\"\n- Element IDs and Types:\n  - `write-review-page` (Div)\n  - `book-info-display` (Div)\n  - `rating-input` (Dropdown/select)\n  - `review-text` (Textarea)\n  - `submit-review-button` (Button)\n  - `back-to-book` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - If editing: `review` (dict) with keys: `review_id`(int), `book_id`(int), `rating`(int), `review_text`(str), `book_title`(str)\n  - If writing new: `book` (dict) with keys: `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str)\n- Navigation:\n  - `submit-review-button`: form POST to `submit_review` or `submit_edit_review` depending on context\n  - `back-to-book`: url_for `book_details` with `book_id`\n\n### 9. Payment Confirmation Template\n- Filename: `templates/payment.html`\n- Page Title: \"Payment Confirmation\"\n- Element IDs and Types:\n  - `payment-page` (Div)\n  - `fine-amount-display` (Div)\n  - `confirm-payment-button` (Button)\n  - `back-to-profile` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `fine_amount` (float)\n- Navigation:\n  - `confirm-payment-button`: form POST to `confirm_payment` with `fine_id`\n  - `back-to-profile`: url_for `user_profile`\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data File Schemas (Backend Development)\n\n### 1. users.txt\n- File Path: `data/users.txt`\n- Fields (pipe-delimited):\n  - `username` (str)\n  - `email` (str)\n  - `phone` (str)\n  - `address` (str)\n- Description: Stores user profile information.\n- Example Rows:\n  - `john_reader|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St`\n  - `jane_doe|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak St`\n\n### 2. books.txt\n- File Path: `data/books.txt`\n- Fields (pipe-delimited):\n  - `book_id` (int)\n  - `title` (str)\n  - `author` (str)\n  - `isbn` (str)\n  - `genre` (str)\n  - `publisher` (str)\n  - `year` (int)\n  - `description` (str)\n  - `status` (str) - \"Available\", \"Borrowed\", \"Reserved\"\n  - `avg_rating` (float)\n- Description: Stores book details including availability and average rating.\n- Example Rows:\n  - `1|To Kill a Mockingbird|Harper Lee|978-0-06-112008-4|Fiction|HarperCollins|1960|A gripping tale of racial injustice and childhood innocence.|Available|4.8`\n  - `2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|978-0-06-231609-7|Non-Fiction|Harper|2011|A brief history of humankind.|Borrowed|4.6`\n  - `3|1984|George Orwell|978-0-452-28423-4|Fiction|Signet Classic|1949|A dystopian social science fiction novel.|Available|4.7`\n\n### 3. borrowings.txt\n- File Path: `data/borrowings.txt`\n- Fields (pipe-delimited):\n  - `borrow_id` (int)\n  - `username` (str)\n  - `book_id` (int)\n  - `borrow_date` (str) (format YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - `due_date` (str) (format YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - `return_date` (str or empty) (format YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - `status` (str) - \"Active\", \"Returned\", \"Overdue\"\n  - `fine_amount` (float)\n- Description: Records borrow transactions and status.\n- Example Rows:\n  - `1|john_reader|2|2024-11-01|2024-11-15||Active|0`\n  - `2|jane_doe|1|2024-10-20|2024-11-03|2024-11-02|Returned|0`\n  - `3|john_reader|3|2024-10-15|2024-10-29||Overdue|5.00`\n\n### 4. reservations.txt\n- File Path: `data/reservations.txt`\n- Fields (pipe-delimited):\n  - `reservation_id` (int)\n  - `username` (str)\n  - `book_id` (int)\n  - `reservation_date` (str) (format YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - `status` (str) - e.g., \"Active\", \"Cancelled\"\n- Description: Stores user book reservations.\n- Example Rows:\n  - `1|jane_doe|4|2024-11-10|Active`\n  - `2|john_reader|2|2024-10-25|Cancelled`\n\n### 5. reviews.txt\n- File Path: `data/reviews.txt`\n- Fields (pipe-delimited):\n  - `review_id` (int)\n  - `username` (str)\n  - `book_id` (int)\n  - `rating` (int) (1-5)\n  - `review_text` (str)\n  - `review_date` (str) (format YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Description: Contains user reviews for books.\n- Example Rows:\n  - `1|jane_doe|1|5|An absolute masterpiece! A must-read.|2024-11-03`\n  - `2|john_reader|3|4|Thought-provoking and eerily relevant today.|2024-10-20`\n\n### 6. fines.txt\n- File Path: `data/fines.txt`\n- Fields (pipe-delimited):\n  - `fine_id` (int)\n  - `username` (str)\n  - `borrow_id` (int)\n  - `amount` (float)\n  - `status` (str) - \"Unpaid\", \"Paid\"\n  - `date_issued` (str) (format YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Description: Records fines issued for overdue borrowings.\n- Example Rows:\n  - `1|john_reader|3|5.00|Unpaid|2024-10-30`\n\n---\n\n# End of Design Specification Document\n\n",

         === design_spec.md ===
         # Design Specification Document for OnlineLibrary
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (Backend Development)
         
         ### 1. Root Route
         - URL Path: `/`
         - Function Name: `root_redirect`
         - HTTP Method: GET
         - Template Rendered: Redirect to `dashboard`
         - Context Variables: None
         
         ### 2. Dashboard Page
         - URL Path: `/dashboard`
         - Function Name: `dashboard`
         - HTTP Method: GET
         - Template Rendered: `dashboard.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `username` (str): Logged-in user's username
           - `featured_books` (list of dict): List of featured books on dashboard; each dict with keys:
             - `book_id` (int)
             - `title` (str)
             - `author` (str)
             - `status` (str) - one of "Available", "Borrowed", "Reserved"
         
         ### 3. Book Catalog Page
         - URL Path: `/catalog`
         - Function Name: `book_catalog`
         - HTTP Method: GET
         - Template Rendered: `catalog.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `books` (list of dict): List of books; each dict has keys:
             - `book_id` (int)
             - `title` (str)
             - `author` (str)
             - `status` (str)
         
         ### 4. Book Details Page
         - URL Path: `/book/<int:book_id>`
         - Function Name: `book_details`
         - HTTP Method: GET
         - Template Rendered: `book_details.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `book` (dict): Book information with keys:
             - `book_id` (int)
             - `title` (str)
             - `author` (str)
             - `status` (str)
             - `description` (str)
             - `avg_rating` (float)
           - `reviews` (list of dict): List of review dicts with keys:
             - `review_id` (int)
             - `username` (str)
             - `rating` (int)
             - `review_text` (str)
             - `review_date` (str) (format YYYY-MM-DD)
         
         ### 5. Borrow Confirmation Page
         - URL Path: `/borrow/<int:book_id>`
         - Function Name: `borrow_confirmation`
         - HTTP Method: GET
         - Template Rendered: `borrow.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `book` (dict): Book info as in `book_details`
           - `due_date` (str): Due date string 14 days from current date (format YYYY-MM-DD)
         
         - URL Path: `/borrow/<int:book_id>/confirm`
         - Function Name: `confirm_borrow`
         - HTTP Method: POST
         - Template Rendered: Redirect or confirmation page as needed (not rendering borrow.html again)
         - Context Variables: None
         
         - URL Path: `/borrow/<int:book_id>/cancel`
         - Function Name: `cancel_borrow`
         - HTTP Method: POST
         - Template Rendered: Redirect to `book_details` page
         - Context Variables: None
         
         ### 6. My Borrowings Page
         - URL Path: `/my_borrows`
         - Function Name: `my_borrows`
         - HTTP Method: GET
         - Template Rendered: `my_borrows.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `borrows` (list of dict): List of borrowings with keys:
             - `borrow_id` (int)
             - `book_title` (str)
             - `borrow_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)
             - `due_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)
             - `status` (str) - e.g., Active, Returned, Overdue
           - `filter_status` (str): The current filter selected (All, Active, Returned, Overdue)
         
         - URL Path: `/return/<int:borrow_id>`
         - Function Name: `return_book`
         - HTTP Method: POST
         - Template Rendered: Redirect or confirmation page
         - Context Variables: None
         
         ### 7. My Reservations Page
         - URL Path: `/my_reservations`
         - Function Name: `my_reservations`
         - HTTP Method: GET
         - Template Rendered: `my_reservations.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `reservations` (list of dict): List of reservations with keys:
             - `reservation_id` (int)
             - `book_title` (str)
             - `reservation_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)
             - `status` (str) - e.g., Active, Cancelled
         
         - URL Path: `/cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id>`
         - Function Name: `cancel_reservation`
         - HTTP Method: POST
         - Template Rendered: Redirect or confirmation
         - Context Variables: None
         
         ### 8. My Reviews Page
         - URL Path: `/my_reviews`
         - Function Name: `my_reviews`
         - HTTP Method: GET
         - Template Rendered: `my_reviews.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `reviews` (list of dict): List of user reviews with keys:
             - `review_id` (int)
             - `book_title` (str)
             - `rating` (int)
             - `review_text` (str)
         
         - URL Path: `/edit_review/<int:review_id>`
         - Function Name: `edit_review_page`
         - HTTP Method: GET
         - Template Rendered: `write_review.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `review` (dict): Existing review details with keys:
             - `review_id` (int)
             - `book_id` (int)
             - `rating` (int)
             - `review_text` (str)
             - `book_title` (str)
         
         - URL Path: `/edit_review/<int:review_id>/submit`
         - Function Name: `submit_edit_review`
         - HTTP Method: POST
         - Template Rendered: Redirect to `my_reviews` or confirmation
         - Context Variables: None
         
         - URL Path: `/delete_review/<int:review_id>`
         - Function Name: `delete_review`
         - HTTP Method: POST
         - Template Rendered: Redirect to `my_reviews`
         - Context Variables: None
         
         ### 9. Write Review Page
         - URL Path: `/write_review/<int:book_id>`
         - Function Name: `write_review_page`
         - HTTP Method: GET
         - Template Rendered: `write_review.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `book` (dict): Book info with keys:
             - `book_id` (int)
             - `title` (str)
             - `author` (str)
         
         - URL Path: `/write_review/<int:book_id>/submit`
         - Function Name: `submit_review`
         - HTTP Method: POST
         - Template Rendered: Redirect to book details or confirmation
         - Context Variables: None
         
         ### 10. User Profile Page
         - URL Path: `/profile`
         - Function Name: `user_profile`
         - HTTP Method: GET
         - Template Rendered: `profile.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `username` (str)
           - `email` (str)
           - `borrow_history` (list of dict): List of previously borrowed books with keys:
             - `book_title` (str)
             - `borrow_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)
             - `return_date` (str or None)
         
         - URL Path: `/profile/update`
         - Function Name: `update_profile`
         - HTTP Method: POST
         - Template Rendered: Redirect or confirmation
         - Context Variables: None
         
         ### 11. Payment Confirmation Page
         - URL Path: `/payment/<int:fine_id>`
         - Function Name: `payment_confirmation`
         - HTTP Method: GET
         - Template Rendered: `payment.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `fine_amount` (float)
         
         - URL Path: `/payment/<int:fine_id>/confirm`
         - Function Name: `confirm_payment`
         - HTTP Method: POST
         - Template Rendered: Redirect or confirmation
         - Context Variables: None
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (Frontend Development)
         
         ### 1. Dashboard Template
         - Filename: `templates/dashboard.html`
         - Page Title: "Library Dashboard"
         - Element IDs and Types:
           - `dashboard-page` (Div)
           - `welcome-message` (H1)
           - `browse-books-button` (Button)
           - `my-borrows-button` (Button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `username` (str)
           - `featured_books` (list of dict with fields: `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str), `status`(str))
         - Navigation:
           - `browse-books-button`: url_for `book_catalog`
           - `my-borrows-button`: url_for `my_borrows`
         
         ### 2. Book Catalog Template
         - Filename: `templates/catalog.html`
         - Page Title: "Book Catalog"
         - Element IDs and Types:
           - `catalog-page` (Div)
           - `search-input` (Input)
           - `book-grid` (Div)
           - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button) - dynamic for each book
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `books` (list of dict with fields: `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str), `status`(str))
         - Navigation:
           - `view-book-button-{book_id}`: url_for `book_details`, parameter: `book_id`
           - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for `dashboard`
         
         ### 3. Book Details Template
         - Filename: `templates/book_details.html`
         - Page Title: "Book Details"
         - Element IDs and Types:
           - `book-details-page` (Div)
           - `book-title` (H1)
           - `book-author` (Div)
           - `book-status` (Div)
           - `borrow-button` (Button)
           - `reviews-section` (Div)
           - `write-review-button` (Button)
           - `back-to-catalog` (Button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `book` (dict): keys as defined in Section 1
           - `reviews` (list of dict): each dict keys `review_id`(int), `username`(str), `rating`(int), `review_text`(str), `review_date`(str)
         - Navigation:
           - `borrow-button`: url_for `borrow_confirmation`, parameter: `book_id` from `book.book_id`
           - `write-review-button`: url_for `write_review_page`, parameter: `book_id`
           - `back-to-catalog`: url_for `book_catalog`
         
         ### 4. Borrow Confirmation Template
         - Filename: `templates/borrow.html`
         - Page Title: "Borrow Confirmation"
         - Element IDs and Types:
           - `borrow-page` (Div)
           - `borrow-book-info` (Div)
           - `due-date-display` (Div)
           - `confirm-borrow-button` (Button)
           - `cancel-borrow-button` (Button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `book` (dict) with keys as in `book_details`
           - `due_date` (str)
         - Navigation:
           - `confirm-borrow-button`: form POST to `confirm_borrow` with `book_id`
           - `cancel-borrow-button`: form POST to `cancel_borrow` with `book_id`
         
         ### 5. My Borrowings Template
         - Filename: `templates/my_borrows.html`
         - Page Title: "My Borrowings"
         - Element IDs and Types:
           - `my-borrows-page` (Div)
           - `filter-status` (Dropdown/select)
           - `borrows-table` (Table)
           - `return-book-button-{borrow_id}` (Button) - dynamic for each active borrow
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `borrows` (list of dict with keys: `borrow_id`(int), `book_title`(str), `borrow_date`(str), `due_date`(str), `status`(str))
           - `filter_status` (str)
         - Navigation:
           - `return-book-button-{borrow_id}`: form POST to `return_book` with `borrow_id`
           - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for `dashboard`
         
         ### 6. My Reservations Template
         - Filename: `templates/my_reservations.html`
         - Page Title: "My Reservations"
         - Element IDs and Types:
           - `reservations-page` (Div)
           - `reservations-table` (Table)
           - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` (Button) - dynamic per reservation
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `reservations` (list of dict with keys: `reservation_id`(int), `book_title`(str), `reservation_date`(str), `status`(str))
         - Navigation:
           - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}`: form POST to `cancel_reservation` with `reservation_id`
           - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for `dashboard`
         
         ### 7. My Reviews Template

           - `delete-review-button-{review_id}` (Button) - per review
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `reviews` (list of dict with keys: `review_id`(int), `book_title`(str), `rating`(int), `review_text`(str))
         - Navigation:

           - `back-to-dashboard`: url_for `dashboard`
         
         ### 8. Write Review Template

         - Navigation:
           - `submit-review-button`: form POST to `submit_review` or `submit_edit_review` depending on context
           - `back-to-book`: url_for `book_details` with `book_id`

         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data File Schemas (Backend Development)
         
         ### 1. users.txt
         - File Path: `data/users.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-delimited):
           - `username` (str)
           - `email` (str)
           - `phone` (str)
           - `address` (str)
         - Description: Stores user profile information.
         - Example Rows:
           - `john_reader|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St`
           - `jane_doe|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak St`
         
         ### 2. books.txt
         - File Path: `data/books.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-delimited):
           - `book_id` (int)
           - `title` (str)
           - `author` (str)
           - `isbn` (str)
           - `genre` (str)
           - `publisher` (str)
           - `year` (int)
           - `description` (str)
           - `status` (str) - "Available", "Borrowed", "Reserved"
           - `avg_rating` (float)
         - Description: Stores book details including availability and average rating.
         - Example Rows:
           - `1|To Kill a Mockingbird|Harper Lee|978-0-06-112008-4|Fiction|HarperCollins|1960|A gripping tale of racial injustice and childhood innocence.|Available|4.8`
           - `2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|978-0-06-231609-7|Non-Fiction|Harper|2011|A brief history of humankind.|Borrowed|4.6`
           - `3|1984|George Orwell|978-0-452-28423-4|Fiction|Signet Classic|1949|A dystopian social science fiction novel.|Available|4.7`
         
         ### 3. borrowings.txt
         - File Path: `data/borrowings.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-delimited):
           - `borrow_id` (int)
           - `username` (str)
           - `book_id` (int)
           - `borrow_date` (str) (format YYYY-MM-DD)
           - `due_date` (str) (format YYYY-MM-DD)
           - `return_date` (str or empty) (format YYYY-MM-DD)
           - `status` (str) - "Active", "Returned", "Overdue"
           - `fine_amount` (float)
         - Description: Records borrow transactions and status.
         - Example Rows:
           - `1|john_reader|2|2024-11-01|2024-11-15||Active|0`
           - `2|jane_doe|1|2024-10-20|2024-11-03|2024-11-02|Returned|0`
           - `3|john_reader|3|2024-10-15|2024-10-29||Overdue|5.00`
         
         ### 4. reservations.txt
         - File Path: `data/reservations.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-delimited):
           - `reservation_id` (int)
           - `username` (str)
           - `book_id` (int)
           - `reservation_date` (str) (format YYYY-MM-DD)
           - `status` (str) - e.g., "Active", "Cancelled"
         - Description: Stores user book reservations.
         - Example Rows:
           - `1|jane_doe|4|2024-11-10|Active`
           - `2|john_reader|2|2024-10-25|Cancelled`
         
         ### 5. reviews.txt
         - File Path: `data/reviews.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-delimited):
           - `review_id` (int)
           - `username` (str)
           - `book_id` (int)
           - `rating` (int) (1-5)
           - `review_text` (str)
           - `review_date` (str) (format YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Description: Contains user reviews for books.
         - Example Rows:
           - `1|jane_doe|1|5|An absolute masterpiece! A must-read.|2024-11-03`
           - `2|john_reader|3|4|Thought-provoking and eerily relevant today.|2024-10-20`
         
         ### 6. fines.txt
         - File Path: `data/fines.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-delimited):
           - `fine_id` (int)
           - `username` (str)
           - `borrow_id` (int)
           - `amount` (float)
           - `status` (str) - "Unpaid", "Paid"
           - `date_issued` (str) (format YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Description: Records fines issued for overdue borrowings.
         - Example Rows:
           - `1|john_reader|3|5.00|Unpaid|2024-10-30`
         
         ---
         
         # End of Design Specification Document

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request, flash
         import os
         from datetime import datetime, timedelta
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'your_secret_key_here'  # Replace with a real secret key
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         
         # === Helper functions to load and save data files ===
         
         def read_users():
             users = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'users.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return users
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line = line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 4:
                         continue
                     users.append({
                         'username': parts[0],
                         'email': parts[1],
                         'phone': parts[2],
                         'address': parts[3],
                     })
             return users
         
         def write_users(users):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'users.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for u in users:
                     fields = [u['username'], u['email'], u['phone'], u['address']]
                     f.write('|'.join(fields) + '\n')
         
         
         def read_books():
             books = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'books.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return books
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line = line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 10:
                         continue
                     try:
                         book = {
                             'book_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'title': parts[1],
                             'author': parts[2],
                             'isbn': parts[3],
                             'genre': parts[4],
                             'publisher': parts[5],
                             'year': int(parts[6]),
                             'description': parts[7],
                             'status': parts[8],
                             'avg_rating': float(parts[9]),
                         }
                         books.append(book)
                     except Exception:
                         continue
             return books
         
         def write_books(books):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'books.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for b in books:
                     fields = [
                         str(b['book_id']),
                         b['title'],
                         b['author'],
                         b['isbn'],
                         b['genre'],
                         b['publisher'],
                         str(b['year']),
                         b['description'],
                         b['status'],
                         f'{b["avg_rating"]:.1f}'
                     ]
                     f.write('|'.join(fields) + '\n')
         
         
         def read_borrowings():
             borrowings = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'borrowings.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return borrowings
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line = line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 8:
                         continue
                     try:
                         borrow = {
                             'borrow_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'username': parts[1],
                             'book_id': int(parts[2]),
                             'borrow_date': parts[3],
                             'due_date': parts[4],
                             'return_date': parts[5] if parts[5] != '' else None,
                             'status': parts[6],
                             'fine_amount': float(parts[7])
                         }
                         borrowings.append(borrow)
                     except Exception:
                         continue
             return borrowings
         
         
         def write_borrowings(borrowings):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'borrowings.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for b in borrowings:
                     fields = [
                         str(b['borrow_id']),
                         b['username'],
                         str(b['book_id']),
                         b['borrow_date'],
                         b['due_date'],
                         b['return_date'] if b['return_date'] else '',
                         b['status'],
                         f'{b["fine_amount"]:.2f}'
                     ]
                     f.write('|'.join(fields) + '\n')

         def write_reservations(reservations):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reservations.txt')

         def read_reviews():
             reviews = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reviews.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return reviews
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line = line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 6:
                         continue
                     try:
                         review = {
                             'review_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'username': parts[1],
                             'book_id': int(parts[2]),
                             'rating': int(parts[3]),
                             'review_text': parts[4],
                             'review_date': parts[5]
                         }
                         reviews.append(review)
                     except Exception:
                         continue
             return reviews
         
         
         def write_reviews(reviews):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reviews.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for r in reviews:
                     fields = [
                         str(r['review_id']),
                         r['username'],
                         str(r['book_id']),
                         str(r['rating']),
                         r['review_text'],
                         r['review_date']
                     ]
                     f.write('|'.join(fields) + '\n')
         
         
         def read_fines():
             fines = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'fines.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return fines
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line = line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 6:
                         continue
                     try:
                         fine = {
                             'fine_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'username': parts[1],
                             'borrow_id': int(parts[2]),
                             'amount': float(parts[3]),
                             'status': parts[4],
                             'date_issued': parts[5]
                         }
                         fines.append(fine)
                     except Exception:
                         continue
             return fines
         
         
         def write_fines(fines):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'fines.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for fin in fines:
                     fields = [
                         str(fin['fine_id']),
                         fin['username'],
                         str(fin['borrow_id']),
                         f'{fin["amount"]:.2f}',
                         fin['status'],
                         fin['date_issued']
                     ]
                     f.write('|'.join(fields) + '\n')
         
         
         # === Mock current logged in user for the purpose of this backend implementation ===
         # For testing/demo, we use a fixed user. In a real app, use auth system.
         CURRENT_USERNAME = 'john_reader'
         
         # === Business helpers ===
         
         def find_user(username):
             users = read_users()
             for u in users:
                 if u['username'] == username:
                     return u
             return None
         
         
         def find_book(book_id):
             books = read_books()
             for b in books:
                 if b['book_id'] == book_id:
                     return b
             return None
         
         
         def update_book_status(book_id, new_status):
             books = read_books()
             updated = False
             for b in books:
                 if b['book_id'] == book_id:
                     b['status'] = new_status
                     updated = True
                     break
             if updated:
                 write_books(books)
         
         
         def next_borrow_id():
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             if not borrowings:
                 return 1
             return max(b['borrow_id'] for b in borrowings) + 1
         
         
         def next_reservation_id():
             reservations = read_reservations()
             if not reservations:
                 return 1
             return max(r['reservation_id'] for r in reservations) + 1
         
         
         def next_review_id():
             reviews = read_reviews()
             if not reviews:
                 return 1
             return max(r['review_id'] for r in reviews) + 1
         
         
         def next_fine_id():
             fines = read_fines()
             if not fines:
                 return 1
             return max(f['fine_id'] for f in fines) + 1
         
         
         def calculate_due_date(borrow_date_str):
             borrow_date = datetime.strptime(borrow_date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')
             due_date = borrow_date + timedelta(days=14)
             return due_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
         
         
         def calculate_fine(due_date_str, return_date_str):
             due_date = datetime.strptime(due_date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')
             return_date = datetime.strptime(return_date_str, '%Y-%m-%d')
             if return_date <= due_date:
                 return 0.0
             # Let's say $1 per day late
             days_late = (return_date - due_date).days
             return float(days_late) * 1.0
         
         
         def update_borrowings_status_and_fines():
             # Update status to Overdue if past due_date and not returned
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             fines = read_fines()
             now = datetime.now()
             fines_changed = False
             borrowings_changed = False
         
             for b in borrowings:
                 if b['status'] == 'Active':
                     due_date_dt = datetime.strptime(b['due_date'], '%Y-%m-%d')
                     if now.date() > due_date_dt.date():
                         # Mark as overdue
                         b['status'] = 'Overdue'
                         # Calculate fine
                         fine_amount = calculate_fine(b['due_date'], now.strftime('%Y-%m-%d'))
                         b['fine_amount'] = fine_amount
                         borrowings_changed = True
         
                         # Check if fine entry exists
                         fine_exists = False
                         for f in fines:
                             if f['borrow_id'] == b['borrow_id'] and f['status'] == 'Unpaid':
                                 fine_exists = True
                                 f['amount'] = fine_amount
                                 break
                         if not fine_exists and fine_amount > 0:
                             # Create new fine
                             new_fine = {
                                 'fine_id': next_fine_id(),
                                 'username': b['username'],
                                 'borrow_id': b['borrow_id'],
                                 'amount': fine_amount,
                                 'status': 'Unpaid',
                                 'date_issued': now.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
                             }
                             fines.append(new_fine)
                             fines_changed = True
         
             if borrowings_changed:
                 write_borrowings(borrowings)
             if fines_changed:
                 write_fines(fines)
         
         
         # === Routes Implementation ===
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             username = CURRENT_USERNAME
             books = read_books()
             # Select featured books arbitrarily - let's pick first 5 or all
             featured_books = []
             count = 0
             for b in books:
                 featured_books.append({
                     'book_id': b['book_id'],
                     'title': b['title'],
                     'author': b['author'],
                     'status': b['status']
                 })
                 count += 1
                 if count >= 5:
                     break
             return render_template('dashboard.html', username=username, featured_books=featured_books)
         
         
         @app.route('/catalog')
         def book_catalog():
             books = read_books()
             books_list = []
             for b in books:
                 books_list.append({
                     'book_id': b['book_id'],
                     'title': b['title'],
                     'author': b['author'],
                     'status': b['status']
                 })
             return render_template('catalog.html', books=books_list)
         
         
         @app.route('/book/<int:book_id>')
         def book_details(book_id):
             book = find_book(book_id)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))
         
             reviews_all = read_reviews()
             reviews_for_book = []
             for r in reviews_all:
                 if r['book_id'] == book_id:
                     reviews_for_book.append({
                         'review_id': r['review_id'],
                         'username': r['username'],
                         'rating': r['rating'],
                         'review_text': r['review_text'],
                         'review_date': r['review_date']
                     })
         
             # Calculate average rating freshly from reviews if any present, else from book data
             if reviews_for_book:
                 avg_rating = round(sum(r['rating'] for r in reviews_for_book) / len(reviews_for_book), 1)
             else:
                 avg_rating = book.get('avg_rating', 0.0)
         
             book_info = {
                 'book_id': book['book_id'],
                 'title': book['title'],
                 'author': book['author'],
                 'status': book['status'],
                 'description': book['description'],
                 'avg_rating': avg_rating
             }
         
             return render_template('book_details.html', book=book_info, reviews=reviews_for_book)
         
         
         @app.route('/borrow/<int:book_id>')
         def borrow_confirmation(book_id):
             book = find_book(book_id)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))
             if book['status'] != 'Available':
                 flash('Book is not available to borrow.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))
         
             due_date = (datetime.now() + timedelta(days=14)).strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
         
             book_info = {
                 'book_id': book['book_id'],
                 'title': book['title'],
                 'author': book['author'],
                 'status': book['status'],
                 'description': book['description'],
                 'avg_rating': book['avg_rating']
             }
         
             return render_template('borrow.html', book=book_info, due_date=due_date)
         
         
         @app.route('/borrow/<int:book_id>/confirm', methods=['POST'])
         def confirm_borrow(book_id):
             book = find_book(book_id)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))
         
             if book['status'] != 'Available':
                 flash('Book is not available to borrow.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))
         
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             new_borrow_id = next_borrow_id()
             borrow_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             due_date = (datetime.now() + timedelta(days=14)).strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             new_borrow = {
                 'borrow_id': new_borrow_id,
                 'username': CURRENT_USERNAME,
                 'book_id': book_id,
                 'borrow_date': borrow_date,
                 'due_date': due_date,
                 'return_date': None,
                 'status': 'Active',
                 'fine_amount': 0.0
             }
             borrowings.append(new_borrow)
             write_borrowings(borrowings)
         
             # Update book status to Borrowed
             update_book_status(book_id, 'Borrowed')
         
             flash('You have successfully borrowed the book.')
             return redirect(url_for('my_borrows'))
         
         
         @app.route('/borrow/<int:book_id>/cancel', methods=['POST'])
         def cancel_borrow(book_id):
             # Simply redirect back to book details
             return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))
         
         
         @app.route('/my_borrows')
         def my_borrows():
             update_borrowings_status_and_fines()
         
             filter_status = request.args.get('filter', 'All')
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             books = read_books()
         
             filtered_borrows = []
             for b in borrowings:
                 if b['username'] != CURRENT_USERNAME:
                     continue
                 # Filter by status if not 'All'
                 if filter_status != 'All' and b['status'] != filter_status:
                     continue
                 # Get book title
                 book_title = next((bk['title'] for bk in books if bk['book_id'] == b['book_id']), 'Unknown')
                 borrow_entry = {
                     'borrow_id': b['borrow_id'],
                     'book_title': book_title,
                     'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],
                     'due_date': b['due_date'],
                     'status': b['status']
                 }
                 filtered_borrows.append(borrow_entry)
         
             return render_template('my_borrows.html', borrows=filtered_borrows, filter_status=filter_status)
         
         
         @app.route('/return/<int:borrow_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def return_book(borrow_id):
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             borrow_found = False
             for b in borrowings:
                 if b['borrow_id'] == borrow_id and b['username'] == CURRENT_USERNAME:
                     if b['status'] not in ['Active', 'Overdue']:
                         flash('Borrow record not active or already returned.')
                         return redirect(url_for('my_borrows'))
                     b['return_date'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
                     b['status'] = 'Returned'
                     b['fine_amount'] = 0.0
                     borrow_found = True
                     # Update book status to Available
                     update_book_status(b['book_id'], 'Available')
                     break
             if borrow_found:
                 write_borrowings(borrowings)
                 flash('Book returned successfully.')
             else:
                 flash('Borrow record not found.')
         
             return redirect(url_for('my_borrows'))
         
         
         @app.route('/my_reservations')
         def my_reservations():
             reservations = read_reservations()
             books = read_books()
             my_reservations_list = []
             for r in reservations:
                 if r['username'] != CURRENT_USERNAME:
                     continue
                 book_title = next((b['title'] for b in books if b['book_id'] == r['book_id']), 'Unknown')
                 my_reservations_list.append({
                     'reservation_id': r['reservation_id'],
                     'book_title': book_title,
                     'reservation_date': r['reservation_date'],
                     'status': r['status']
                 })
             return render_template('my_reservations.html', reservations=my_reservations_list)
         
         
         @app.route('/cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def cancel_reservation(reservation_id):
             reservations = read_reservations()
             changed = False
             for r in reservations:
                 if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id and r['username'] == CURRENT_USERNAME:
                     if r['status'] == 'Active':
                         r['status'] = 'Cancelled'
                         changed = True
                         break
             if changed:
                 write_reservations(reservations)
                 flash('Reservation cancelled.')
             else:
                 flash('Reservation not found or already cancelled.')
             return redirect(url_for('my_reservations'))
         
         
         @app.route('/my_reviews')
         def my_reviews():
             reviews_all = read_reviews()
             books = read_books()
             user_reviews = []
             for r in reviews_all:
                 if r['username'] == CURRENT_USERNAME:
                     book_title = next((b['title'] for b in books if b['book_id'] == r['book_id']), 'Unknown')
                     user_reviews.append({
                         'review_id': r['review_id'],
                         'book_title': book_title,
                         'rating': r['rating'],
                         'review_text': r['review_text']
                     })
             return render_template('my_reviews.html', reviews=user_reviews)
         
         
         @app.route('/edit_review/<int:review_id>')
         def edit_review_page(review_id):
             reviews_all = read_reviews()
             review = None
             for r in reviews_all:
                 if r['review_id'] == review_id and r['username'] == CURRENT_USERNAME:
                     review = r
                     break
             if not review:
                 flash('Review not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))
             books = read_books()
             book_title = next((b['title'] for b in books if b['book_id'] == review['book_id']), 'Unknown')
             review_context = {
                 'review_id': review['review_id'],
                 'book_id': review['book_id'],
                 'rating': review['rating'],
                 'review_text': review['review_text'],
                 'book_title': book_title
             }
             return render_template('write_review.html', review=review_context)
         
         
         @app.route('/edit_review/<int:review_id>/submit', methods=['POST'])
         def submit_edit_review(review_id):
             rating = request.form.get('rating')
             review_text = request.form.get('review_text', '').strip()
             if not rating or not review_text:
                 flash('Rating and review text are required.')
                 return redirect(url_for('edit_review_page', review_id=review_id))
             try:
                 rating_val = int(rating)
                 if rating_val < 1 or rating_val > 5:
                     raise ValueError
             except ValueError:
                 flash('Invalid rating value.')
                 return redirect(url_for('edit_review_page', review_id=review_id))
         
             reviews_all = read_reviews()
             changed = False
             for r in reviews_all:
                 if r['review_id'] == review_id and r['username'] == CURRENT_USERNAME:
                     r['rating'] = rating_val
                     r['review_text'] = review_text
                     r['review_date'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
                     changed = True
                     break
             if changed:
                 write_reviews(reviews_all)
                 flash('Review updated successfully.')
             else:
                 flash('Review not found.')
             return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))
         
         
         @app.route('/delete_review/<int:review_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def delete_review(review_id):
             reviews_all = read_reviews()
             new_reviews = []
             deleted = False
             for r in reviews_all:
                 if r['review_id'] == review_id and r['username'] == CURRENT_USERNAME:
                     deleted = True
                     continue
                 new_reviews.append(r)
             if deleted:
                 write_reviews(new_reviews)
                 flash('Review deleted successfully.')
             else:
                 flash('Review not found.')
             return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))
         
         
         @app.route('/write_review/<int:book_id>')
         def write_review_page(book_id):
             book = find_book(book_id)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))
             book_info = {
                 'book_id': book['book_id'],
                 'title': book['title'],
                 'author': book['author']
             }
             return render_template('write_review.html', book=book_info)
         
         
         @app.route('/write_review/<int:book_id>/submit', methods=['POST'])
         def submit_review(book_id):
             rating = request.form.get('rating')
             review_text = request.form.get('review_text', '').strip()
             if not rating or not review_text:
                 flash('Rating and review text are required.')
                 return redirect(url_for('write_review_page', book_id=book_id))
             try:
                 rating_val = int(rating)
                 if rating_val < 1 or rating_val > 5:
                     raise ValueError
             except ValueError:
                 flash('Invalid rating value.')
                 return redirect(url_for('write_review_page', book_id=book_id))
         
             reviews_all = read_reviews()
             new_review_id = next_review_id()
             new_review = {
                 'review_id': new_review_id,
                 'username': CURRENT_USERNAME,
                 'book_id': book_id,
                 'rating': rating_val,
                 'review_text': review_text,
                 'review_date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             }
             reviews_all.append(new_review)
             write_reviews(reviews_all)
         
             flash('Review submitted successfully.')
             return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))
         
         
         @app.route('/profile')
         def user_profile():
             user = find_user(CURRENT_USERNAME)
             if not user:
                 flash('User not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             books = read_books()
         
             borrow_history = []
             for b in borrowings:
                 if b['username'] != CURRENT_USERNAME:
                     continue
                 # Only include returned or overdue borrowings?
                 if b['status'] in ['Returned', 'Overdue', 'Active']:
                     book_title = next((bk['title'] for bk in books if bk['book_id'] == b['book_id']), 'Unknown')
                     borrow_history.append({
                         'book_title': book_title,
                         'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],
                         'return_date': b['return_date'] if b['return_date'] else None
                     })
         
             return render_template('profile.html', username=user['username'], email=user['email'], borrow_history=borrow_history)
         
         
         @app.route('/profile/update', methods=['POST'])
         def update_profile():
             email = request.form.get('email')
             phone = request.form.get('phone')
             address = request.form.get('address')
         
             users = read_users()
             updated = False
             for u in users:
                 if u['username'] == CURRENT_USERNAME:
                     if email:
                         u['email'] = email
                     if phone:
                         u['phone'] = phone
                     if address:
                         u['address'] = address
                     updated = True
                     break
             if updated:
                 write_users(users)
                 flash('Profile updated successfully.')
             else:
                 flash('User not found.')
         
             return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))
         
         
         @app.route('/payment/<int:fine_id>')
         def payment_confirmation(fine_id):
             fines = read_fines()
             fine_amount = None
             for f in fines:
                 if f['fine_id'] == fine_id and f['username'] == CURRENT_USERNAME and f['status'] == 'Unpaid':
                     fine_amount = f['amount']
                     break
             if fine_amount is None:
                 flash('Fine not found or already paid.')
                 return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))
             return render_template('payment.html', fine_amount=fine_amount)
         
         
         @app.route('/payment/<int:fine_id>/confirm', methods=['POST'])
         def confirm_payment(fine_id):
             fines = read_fines()
             changed = False
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             for f in fines:
                 if f['fine_id'] == fine_id and f['username'] == CURRENT_USERNAME and f['status'] == 'Unpaid':
                     f['status'] = 'Paid'
                     changed = True
                     # Also update borrowings fine_amount for the related borrow
                     borrow_id = f['borrow_id']
                     for b in borrowings:
                         if b['borrow_id'] == borrow_id:
                             b['fine_amount'] = 0.0
                             break
                     break
             if changed:
                 write_fines(fines)
                 write_borrowings(borrowings)
                 flash('Payment successful.')
             else:
                 flash('Fine not found or already paid.')
         
             return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)
